          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I have installed Node.js modules by 'npm install', and then I tried to do
            <code>
             gulp sass-watch
            </code>
            in a command prompt. After that, I got the below response.
           </p>
           <pre class="lang-none prettyprint-override"><code>[18:18:32] Requiring external module babel-register
fs.js:27
const { Math, Object, Reflect } = primordials;
                                  ^

ReferenceError: primordials is not defined
</code></pre>
           <p>
            I have tried this before
            <code>
             gulp sass-watch
            </code>
            :
           </p>
           <pre class="lang-none prettyprint-override"><code>npm -g install gulp-cli
</code></pre>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">
            <div class="d-flex ps-relative fw-wrap">
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/node.js" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'node.js'">
              node.js
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/sass" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'sass'">
              sass
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/gulp" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'gulp'">
              gulp
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/gulp-sass" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'gulp-sass'">
              gulp-sass
             </a>
            </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="55926692">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/55926692/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I hit the same error. I suspect you're using Node.js 12 and Gulp.js 3. That combination does not work:
             <em>
              <a href="https://github.com/gulpjs/gulp/issues/2324" rel="noreferrer">
               Gulp.js 3 is broken on Node.js 12 #2324
              </a>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             A previous workaround from Jan. does not work either:
             <em>
              <a href="https://github.com/gulpjs/gulp/issues/2246" rel="noreferrer">
               After update to Node.js 11.0.0 running Gulp.js exits with 'ReferenceError: internalBinding is not defined' #2246
              </a>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             Solution: Either upgrade to Gulp.js 4 or downgrade to an earlier version of Node.js.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="58394828" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="2" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="741" id="answer-58394828" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58394828">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="741" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             741
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

               </path>

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58394828/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             We encountered the same issue when updating a legacy project depending on
             <code>
              gulp@3.9.1
             </code>
             to Node.js 12+.
            </p>
            <p>
             These fixes enable you to use Node.js 12+ with
             <code>
              gulp@3.9.1
             </code>
             by overriding
             <code>
              graceful-fs
             </code>
             to version
             <code>
              ^4.2.9
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <h2>
             If you are using yarn v1
            </h2>
            <p>
             Yarn v1
             <a href="https://classic.yarnpkg.com/en/docs/selective-version-resolutions/" rel="noreferrer">
              supports resolving a package to a defined version
             </a>
             .
You need to add a
             <code>
              resolutions
             </code>
             section to your
             <code>
              package.json
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-json prettyprint-override"><code>{
  // Your current package.json contents
  "resolutions": {
    "graceful-fs": "^4.2.9"
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Thanks
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/1650473/jazd">
              @jazd
             </a>
             for this way to solve the issue.
            </p>
            <h2>
             If you are using npm &gt;= 8.3.0
            </h2>
            <p>
             <code>
              npm@^8.3.0
             </code>
             enables you to override the version of a package of your project's dependencies. To do so, you should add
             <a href="https://docs.npmjs.com/cli/v8/configuring-npm/package-json#overrides" rel="noreferrer">
              an
              <code>
               overrides
              </code>
              section
             </a>
             in your package.json:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-json prettyprint-override"><code>{
  // Your current package.json
  "overrides": {
    "graceful-fs": "^4.2.9"
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <h2>
             If you are using npm &lt; 8.3.0
            </h2>
            <p>
             Using
             <a href="https://github.com/rogeriochaves/npm-force-resolutions" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               npm-force-resolutions
              </code>
             </a>
             as a preinstall script, you can obtain a similar result as with yarn v1. You need to modify your package.json this way:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-json prettyprint-override"><code>{
  // Your current package.json
  "scripts": {
    // Your current package.json scripts
    "preinstall": "npx npm-force-resolutions"
  },
  "resolutions": {
    "graceful-fs": "^4.2.9"
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <code>
              npm-force-resolutions
             </code>
             will alter the
             <code>
              package-lock.json
             </code>
             file to set
             <code>
              graceful-fs
             </code>
             to the wanted version before the
             <code>
              install
             </code>
             is done.
            </p>
            <p>
             If you are using a custom
             <code>
              .npmrc
             </code>
             file in your project and it contains either a proxy or custom registry, you might need to change
             <code>
              npx npm-force-resolutions
             </code>
             to
             <code>
              npx --userconfig .npmrc npm-force-resolutions
             </code>
             because as of now,
             <code>
              npx
             </code>
             doesn't use the current folder
             <code>
              .npmrc
             </code>
             file by default.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Origin of the problem
            </h2>
            <p>
             This issue stems from the fact that
             <code>
              gulp@3.9.1
             </code>
             <a href="https://github.com/gulpjs/gulp/blob/v3.9.1/package.json#L47" rel="noreferrer">
              depends
             </a>
             on
             <code>
              graceful-fs@^3.0.0
             </code>
             which monkeypatches Node.js
             <code>
              fs
             </code>
             module.
            </p>
            <p>
             This used to work with Node.js until version 11.15 (which is a
             <a href="https://nodejs.org/en/about/releases/" rel="noreferrer">
              version
             </a>
             from a development branch and shouldn't be used in production).
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://github.com/isaacs/node-graceful-fs#v4" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               graceful-fs@^4.0.0
              </code>
             </a>
             does not monkeypatch Node.js
             <code>
              fs
             </code>
             module anymore, which makes it compatible with Node.js &gt; 11.15 (tested and working with versions 12 and 14).
            </p>
            <p>
             Note that this is not a perennial solution but it helps when you don't have the time to update to
             <code>
              gulp@^4.0.0
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 If you use yarn (v1) you can add this to your resolutions in your package.json to achieve the same thing -
                 <code>
                  "**/graceful-fs": "^4.0.0"
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h1>
             Fix it in one minute:
            </h1>
            <p>
             Just follow
             <a href="https://timonweb.com/posts/how-to-fix-referenceerror-primordials-is-not-defined-error/" rel="noreferrer">
              these steps
             </a>
             . I'm on Windows 10 and it worked perfectly for me!
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               In the same directory where you have
               <code>
                package.json
               </code>
               create a
               <code>
                npm-shrinkwrap.json
               </code>
               file with the following contents:
              </p>
              <pre><code>    {
      "dependencies": {
        "graceful-fs": {
            "version": "4.2.2"
         }
      }
    }
</code></pre>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Run
               <code>
                npm install
               </code>
               , and don't worry, it will update
               <code>
                npm-shrinkwrap.json
               </code>
               with a bunch of content.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Run
               <code>
                gulp
               </code>
               to start the project.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="57804190">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use the following commands and install
             <strong>
              Node.js v11.15.0
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-bash prettyprint-override"><code>npm install -g n

sudo n 11.15.0
</code></pre>
            <p>
             will solve
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              ReferenceError: primordials is not defined in node
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Referred from @Terje Norderhaug @Tom Corelis answers.
            </p>

             <time datetime="2019-09-05T11:11:03" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="57804190">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58022933">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58022933/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use the following commands to install Node.js v11.15.0 and Gulp.js v3.9.1:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-bash prettyprint-override"><code>npm install -g n

sudo n 11.15.0

npm install gulp@^3.9.1
npm install
npm rebuild node-sass
</code></pre>
            <p>
             It will solve this issue:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              ReferenceError: primordials is not defined in node
             </p>
            </blockquote>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="67384898">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="34" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             34
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/67384898/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For me,
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/55921442/how-to-fix-referenceerror-primordials-is-not-defined-in-node-js/60921145#60921145">
              Diego Fortes' answer
             </a>
             works with one small change.
            </p>
            <p>
             Here is my workflow if this error appears:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               <code>
                npm install
               </code>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               <code>
                npm install gulp
               </code>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               create file
               <em>
                npm-shrinkwrap.json
               </em>
               with
              </p>
              <pre><code>{
  "dependencies": {
    "graceful-fs": {
        "version": "4.2.2"
     }
  }
}
</code></pre>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               <code>
                npm install
               </code>
               (again) (Not
               <code>
                npm install gulp
               </code>
               again! Very important - otherwise the error will be come back)
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               gulp (now working)
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">

           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56328843">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Using
             <a href="https://github.com/nvm-sh/nvm" rel="noreferrer">
              NVM
             </a>
             to manage what Node.js version you're using, running the following commands worked for me:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code>cd /to/your/project/
nvm install lts/dubnium
nvm use lts/dubnium
yarn upgrade # or `npm install`
</code></pre>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="61405958">

            </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/61405958/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Simple and elegant solution
              </strong>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Just follow these steps. It worked perfectly with npm install running multiple times or installing any other modules or even publishing project to artifactory.
            </p>
            <p>
             In the same directory where you have package.json create a
             <strong>
              npm-shrinkwrap.json
             </strong>
             file with the following contents:
            </p>
            <pre><code>{
  "dependencies": {
    "graceful-fs": {
        "version": "4.2.2"
     }
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Run npm install, and don't worry, it'll update npm-shrinkwrap.json with a bunch of content. Let's get rid of this updates by updating
             <strong>
              package.json
             </strong>
             scripts options.
            </p>
            <pre><code>"scripts": {
    "preshrinkwrap": "git checkout -- npm-shrinkwrap.json",
    "postshrinkwrap": "git checkout -- npm-shrinkwrap.json"
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now you can run npm install and your npm-shrinkwrap.json will be intact and will work forever.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="58771749" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="23" id="answer-58771749" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58771749">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58771749/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Gulp 3.9.1 doesn't work with Node v12.x.x, and if you upgrade to Gulp 4.0.2, you have to completely change gulpfile.js with the new syntax (series &amp; parallels). So your best bet is to downgrade to Node.js v 11.x.x (the 11.15.0 version worked fine for me) by simply using the following code in a terminal:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-none prettyprint-override"><code>nvm install 11.15.0
nvm use 11.15.0 # Just in case it didn't automatically select the 11.15.0 as the main node.
nvm uninstall 13.1.0
npm rebuild node-sass
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="60136898">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="60136898" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="23" id="answer-60136898" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="60136898">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="23" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             23
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/60136898/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h1>
             TL:DR
            </h1>
            <p>
             Gulp
             <code>
              3.*
             </code>
             doesn't work on Node.js
             <code>
              12.*
             </code>
             or above. You have to downgrade Node.js, or upgrade Gulp.
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              If you are short on time, downgrade Node.js to v11.* or below; if you need newer features, and have time to possibly fix a load of broken dependencies, upgrade Gulp to 4.* or above!
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             As others have already mentioned, Gulp 3.* is not supported on Node.js 12 or above, so you will have to downgrade your Node version to 11.* or below, OR upgrade your Gulp to 4.0.
            </p>
            <p>
             The best option depends ultimately on how much time you have, as upgrading Gulp brings benefits of cleaner gulpfiles and in-built control over having tasks run in
             <a href="https://gulpjs.com/docs/en/getting-started/creating-tasks" rel="noreferrer">
              series or parallel
             </a>
             , but also relies on you rewriting your gulpfile to a new syntax, and
             <em>
              might
             </em>
             (read: probably will - see end of this comment) cause conflicts with some dependencies.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <h2>
             Downgrading Node.js
            </h2>
            <p>
             This is the easiest and quickest option. Especially if you use
             <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/n" rel="noreferrer">
              n
             </a>
             or
             <a href="https://nvm.sh" rel="noreferrer">
              nvm
             </a>
             , as these allow you to very quick install and switch between Node.js versions.
            </p>
            <h3>
             Installing Node.js version on N
            </h3>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code>n 10.16.0
</code></pre>
            <h3>
             Installing a Node.js version on NVM
            </h3>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code>nvm install 10.16.0
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Once you have done this, you
             <em>
              may
             </em>
             need to rebuild your
             <a href="https://docs.npmjs.com/cli/rebuild" rel="noreferrer">
              npm dependencies
             </a>
             or alternatively remove both your
             <code>
              node_modules
             </code>
             folder
             <em>
              and
             </em>
             your
             <code>
              package-lock.json
             </code>
             file and reinstalling your dependencies. Though if you are merely reverting to a preexisting Node.js version, you should probably be fine.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <h1>
             Upgrading Gulp
            </h1>
            <p>
             As mentioned above, this is a more time-intensive task, but it might bring benefits in the long run. For example, Node.js 12 has now introduced native support for ES Modules (behind an experimental flag) and full support in Node.js 13.
            </p>
            <p>
             You may need to upgrade Node.js to use that, forcing you to upgrade Gulp. Or you may simply want the benefits of using Gulp 4, as it offers better and more efficient control over writing tasks.
            </p>
            <p>
             There are a number of articles on this already, so I won't elaborate any further on the specifics, but to reiterate -
             <strong>
              this is not a quick job
             </strong>
             . Depending on the size of your project, there may be some notable rewriting required, and you may have dependencies that break. If you are in short supply of time, you should opt for simply downgrading Node.js, at least temporarily.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <h2>
             But I already have Gulp 4, and it still doesn't work!
            </h2>
            <p>
             If, like me, you are already using Gulp 4+ (I was using Gulp
             <code>
              4.0.2
             </code>
             , originally on Node.js 10) and have recently upgraded (I upgraded to Node.js 13.8.0) are you are still getting the issue, it may be because a dependency is relying on an older version of Gulp, and that is getting caught in the pipeline.
            </p>
            <p>
             In my case,
             <code>
              gulp-combine-mq
             </code>
             was a dependency using Gulp 3.9.*. Disabling this task in my gulpfile allowed Gulp to run again.
            </p>
            <p>
             If this happens, you have a few options. You can,
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Go without the plugin if it's not absolutely necessary
             </li>
             <li>
              Find an alternative,
             </li>
             <li>
              Fix the plugin
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Needless to say, if you have several plugins that rely on an older version of Gulp - especially if these plugins are vital for your application - this is where there can be a huge additional chunk of time spent in upgrading Gulp (hence the warnings above).
            </p>
            <p>
             If this happens, it is best to just downgrade Node.js, at least until patches can be issued.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

                 <span class="v-visible-sr">
                  15 silver badges
                 </span>
                 <span aria-hidden="true" title="22 bronze badges">
                  <span class="badge3">
                  </span>
                  <span class="badgecount">
                   22
                  </span>

          </span>
          <div class="post-layout--right js-post-comments-component">
           <div class="comments js-comments-container bt bc-black-075 mt12" data-min-length="15" data-post-id="60136898" id="comments-60136898">
            <ul class="comments-list js-comments-list" data-addlink-disabled="true" data-canpost="false" data-cansee="true" data-comments-unavailable="false" data-remaining-comments-count="0">
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="113566923" data-comment-owner-id="1064598" data-comment-score="2" id="comment-113566923">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 2
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 To me, this is also my case. I was using Gulp 4, but a old gulp plugin was internally depending on old graceful-fs version. Culprit can be found using
                 <code>
                  npm ls graceful-fs
                 </code>
                 - a package using graceful-fs with version below 4 will be causing this issue. Remove it from gulpfile, use an alternative or upgrade it to fix the issue.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1064598/ondra-koupil" title="952 reputation">
                  Ondra Koupil
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2020-10-06 09:39:51Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Oct 6, 2020 at 9:39
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had the same error. I finally fixed that when I updated all packages and then mentioned the
             <strong>
              same Node.js engine version and npm version
             </strong>
             in
             <code>
              package.json
             </code>
             as it is in my local working system.
            </p>
            <pre><code> "engines": {
    "node": "10.15.3",
    "npm": "6.9.0"
 }
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I was getting this error when deploying on
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Heroku" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Heroku
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             For more, check out
             <a href="https://devcenter.heroku.com/articles/nodejs-support#specifying-a-node-js-version" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Heroku support
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="62501450" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="12" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-62501450" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="62501450">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/62501450/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Check Node.js version:
            </p>
            <pre><code> node --version
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Check gulp version:
            </p>
            <pre><code>gulp -v
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If Node.js &gt;=12 and gulp &lt;= 3, do one of the following:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Upgrade gulp
             </li>
            </ol>
            <pre><code>sudo npm install -g gulp
</code></pre>
            <ol start="2">
             <li>
              Downgrade node
             </li>
            </ol>
            <pre><code>sudo npm install -g n
sudo n 11.15.0
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <em>
              <a href="https://www.surrealcms.com/blog/how-to-upgrade-or-downgrade-nodejs-using-npm.html" rel="noreferrer">
               How to Upgrade (or Downgrade) Node.js Using npm
              </a>
             </em>
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In case the problem is not from
             <code>
              gulp
             </code>
             then check the
             <a href="https://github.com/EvanOxfeld/node-unzip" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              unzip
             </a>
             npm module. It's been around six years since the last time it was updated. It doesn't work with Node.js &gt; v11.
            </p>
            <p>
             Try this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>npm install -g n

sudo n 11.15.0
</code></pre>
           </div>

            <p>
             Downgrading to Node.js stable fixed this issue for me, as it occurred after I upgraded to Node.js 12:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-bash prettyprint-override"><code>sudo n 10.16.0
</code></pre>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="60313725" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="5" id="answer-60313725" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="60313725">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/60313725/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This error is because of the
             <strong>
              new version of Node.js
             </strong>
             (12) and
             <strong>
              an old version of Gulp
             </strong>
             (less than 4).
            </p>
            <p>
             Downgrading Node.js and other dependencies isn't recommended. I solved this by updating
             <code>
              package.json
             </code>
             file, fetching the latest version of all dependencies. For this, I use
             <code>
              npm-check-updates
             </code>
             . It is a module that updates the
             <code>
              package.json
             </code>
             with the latest version of all dependencies.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Reference
             </strong>
             :
             <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/npm-check-updates" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://www.npmjs.com/package/npm-check-updates
             </a>
            </p>
            <pre><code>npm i -g npm-check-updates
ncu -u
npm install
</code></pre>
            <p>
             In most cases, we will have to update the
             <code>
              gulpfile.js
             </code>
             as well like the following:
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Reference
             </strong>
             :
             <em>
              <a href="https://fettblog.eu/gulp-4-parallel-and-series/#migration" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               Gulp 4: The new task execution system - gulp.parallel and gulp.series, Migration
              </a>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             Before:
            </p>
            <pre><code>gulp.task(
    'sass', function () {
        return gulp.src([sourcePath + '/sass/**/*.scss', "!" + sourcePath + "/sass/**/_*.scss"])

            ....
    }
);

Other configuration...

gulp.task(
    'watch', function () {
        gulp.watch(sourcePath + '/sass/**/*.scss', ['sass']);
    }
);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             After:
            </p>
            <pre><code>gulp.task('sass', gulp.series(function(done) {
    return gulp.src([sourcePath + '/sass/**/*.scss', "!" + sourcePath + "/sass/**/_*.scss"])

            ...

    done();
}));

Other config...

gulp.task(
    'watch', function () {
        gulp.watch(sourcePath + '/sass/**/*.scss', gulp.series('sass'));
    }
);
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="56988925" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="16" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-56988925" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56988925">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56988925/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I faced the same issue. What I tried and what worked for me:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Check the version of
               <em>
                Node.js
               </em>
               and
               <em>
                Gulp.js
               </em>
               (a combination of Node.js v12 and Gulp.js less than v4 doesn't work)
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               I downgraded the NPM version by:
              </p>
              <pre class="lang-bash prettyprint-override"><code>sudo NPM install -g n
sudo n 10.16.0
</code></pre>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             It worked fine. Then just follow the instructions of your console.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="56692504" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="18" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2" id="answer-56692504" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56692504">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56692504/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I was getting this error on Windows 10. It turned out to be a corrupted roaming profile.
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-none prettyprint-override"><code>npm ERR! node v12.4.0
npm ERR! npm  v3.3.12

npm ERR! primordials is not defined
npm ERR!
npm ERR! If you need help, you may report this error at:
npm ERR!     &lt;https://github.com/npm/npm/issues&gt;

npm ERR! Please include the following file with any support request:
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Deleting the
             <code>
              C:\Users\{user}\AppData\Roaming\npm
             </code>
             folder fixed my issue.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="59173763" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2" id="answer-59173763" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="59173763">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/59173763/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If keeping Node.js v12 while using the latest gulp ^4.0, follow these steps:
            </p>
            <p>
             Update the command-line interface (just for precaution) using:
            </p>
            <pre><code>npm i gulp-cli -g
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Add/Update the
             <code>
              gulp
             </code>
             under dependencies section of your
             <em>
              package.json
             </em>
             file
            </p>
            <pre><code>"dependencies": {
  "gulp": "^4.0.0"
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Delete your
             <code>
              package-lock.json
             </code>
             file.
            </p>
            <p>
             Delete your
             <code>
              node_modules
             </code>
             folder.
            </p>
            <p>
             Finally, run
             <code>
              npm i
             </code>
             to upgrade and recreate a brand new
             <em>
              node_modules
             </em>
             folder and
             <em>
              package-lock.json
             </em>
             file with correct parameters for Gulp ^4.0:
            </p>
            <pre><code>npm i
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Note
             </strong>
             Gulp.js 4.0 introduces the
             <code>
              series()
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              parallel()
             </code>
             methods to combine tasks instead of the array methods used in Gulp 3, and so you may or may not encounter an error in your old
             <code>
              gulpfile.js
             </code>
             script.
            </p>
            <p>
             To learn more about applying these new features,
             <a href="https://www.sitepoint.com/how-to-migrate-to-gulp-4/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              this site
             </a>
             have really done justice to it:
             <em>
              <a href="https://www.sitepoint.com/how-to-migrate-to-gulp-4/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               How to Migrate to Gulp.js 4.0
              </a>
             </em>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="59192305">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/59192305/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I fixed this issue on Windows 10 by uninstalling Node.js from
             <em>
              Add or Remove Programs
             </em>
             → Node.js.
            </p>
            <p>
             Then I installed version 11.15.0 from
             <a href="https://nodejs.org/download/release/v11.15.0/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://nodejs.org/download/release/v11.15.0/
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Choose
             <em>
              node-v11.15.0-x64.msi
             </em>
             if you're running Windows 64-bit.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2019-12-05T09:48:20" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="59192305">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Gulp is making issue with Node.js version 11 and above. Uninstall your current Node.js version and reinstall the
             <code>
              v10.15.1
             </code>
             version. Here is the link for that version. This helps me and it will solve your problem too.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://nodejs.org/download/release/v10.15.1/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://nodejs.org/download/release/v10.15.1/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="67018436">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/67018436/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Install gulp and add your Node.js version to the
             <em>
              package.json
             </em>
             file like so:
            </p>
            <pre><code>{
  "dependencies": {
    "node":  "^10.16.3"
  }
}
</code></pre>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="71264617">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/71264617/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The problem occurred for me in Visual Studio's
             <strong>
              Task Runner Explorer
             </strong>
             only and not when running from the command line or PowerShell.
            </p>
            <p>
             I realised that VS was ignoring the Node version I had set with
             <strong>
              NVM
             </strong>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             This post gave the answer:
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/58010389/configure-which-npm-is-used-by-visual-studios-task-runner-explorer">
              Configure which NPM is used by Visual Studio's Task Runner Explorer?
             </a>
             by setting the
             <strong>
              PATH
             </strong>
             variable as a higher priority than external tools in VS, it used the Node version set by NVM and not the version installed with VS.
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1ZR19.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1ZR19.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="66746738" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="24" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-66746738" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="66746738">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/66746738/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had this very same error, but it was caused by a different issue.
            </p>
            <pre><code>OS: windows 10
nodejs version: 15.12.0
npm version: 7.6.3
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The cause of the problem was
             <strong>
              graceful-fs
             </strong>
             package.
Whenever I tried to run npm, even running npm-v was firing "ReferenceError: primordials is not defined".
            </p>
            <p>
             I tried running npm install graceful-fs@latest, but it still didn't work, even though the package was latest version.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              So what helped me?
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             run
             <code>
              npm ls graceful-fs
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             This way you'll find all packages on which
             <code>
              graceful-fs
             </code>
             is dependency and which version it has. In my case it was mostly version 3.0, even though I've installed version 4.2.6
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              So how to fix it?
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Open npm-shrinkwrap.json (not sure about packages-lock.json) and change search for
             <code>
              graceful-fs
             </code>
             - you'll see that it has older versions on a few places. Replace it with
             <code>
              ^4.2.6
             </code>
             (or newer).
            </p>
            <p>
             Then
             <code>
              npm audit fix --force
             </code>
             which will forcefully install the newer version everywhere.
            </p>
            <p>
             Hope this works for you, it took me a few hours to find out how to fix it.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">

           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="59549764">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/59549764/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you're trying to install
             <code>
              semantic-ui
             </code>
             and the following error occurs then try downloading the latest version of Node.js
             <code>
              js(13.5.0)
             </code>
             with the latest features, from Node.js.org.
            </p>
            <p>
             Moreover, rather than trying the NPM install semantic, you should just add the link (which you can find from the
             <a href="https://cdnjs.com/libraries/semantic-ui" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              cdnjs link
             </a>
             ) to the header of your
             <code>
              index.html
             </code>
             file.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="64062494" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="26" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-64062494" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="64062494">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/64062494/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
