          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I have tried a lot of suggestions to fix this problem for an existing project on my Windows 10 machine and ended up following these steps to fix it;
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Uninstall Node.js from "Add or remove programs". Fire up a new Command prompt and type
              <code>
               gulp -v
              </code>
              and then
              <code>
               node -v
              </code>
              to check that it has been uninstalled completely.
             </li>
             <li>
              Download and install Node.js
              <a href="https://nodejs.org/download/release/v10.16.0/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               v10.16.0
              </a>
              - not the latest as latest node &amp; gulp combination is causing the problem as far as I see. During installation I didn't change the installation path which I normally do(C:\Program Files\nodejs).
             </li>
             <li>
              Open up a new Command prompt, go to your project's directory where you have got your gulpfile.js and start gulp as shown in the image.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Please note sometimes when I switch between git branches I might need to close my Visual Studio and run it as Admin again in order to see this solution working again.
            </p>
            <p>
             As far as I see this problem started to happen after I installed the latest recommended version(12.18.4) of Node.js for a new project and I only realised this when some FE changes weren't reflected on the existing web project.
            </p>
            <p>
             Update: Today I had the same problem while setting up one of my existing projects on my new PC and I did the same steps + went to the directory where I have the gulpfile and then run
             <code>
              npm install
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/ZiqgX.jpg" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/ZiqgX.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="60753464" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="27" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-60753464" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="60753464">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/60753464/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This is because the compatibility issue between
             <code>
              node
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              gulp
             </code>
             in your system. Downgrading the
             <code>
              node
             </code>
             or upgrading the
             <code>
              gulp
             </code>
             will fix this issue.
            </p>
            <pre><code>sudo npm i -g n
sudo n 11.15.0
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Try removing the
             <code>
              node_modules
             </code>
             folder and
             <code>
              package-lock.json
             </code>
             file and installing again using
             <code>
              npm i
             </code>
             command if still not working.
            </p>
           </div>

             For those who are using
             <a href="https://yarnpkg.com/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Yarn
             </a>

            </p>
            <pre class="lang-bash prettyprint-override"><code>yarn global add n
n 11.15.0
yarn install # Have to install again

             You have two options here

              Either upgrade to gulp 4 or else
             </li>

              downgrade to an earlier Node.js version.

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I got the same issue installing the npm package
             <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/webshot" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              webshot
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             NOTE: it was a known issue for that package as it depends on graceful-fs behind the scenes.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Fix: 1.
             </strong>
             <strong>
              upgrade graceful-fs  to 4.x or higher
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Fix: 2.
             </strong>
             <strong>
              use webshot-node instead
              <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/webshot-node" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               https://www.npmjs.com/package/webshot-node
              </a>
             </strong>
            </p>
           </div>
